<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Samson
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Samson an oratorio
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="sh">Handel Oratorij Samson</span>; <span title="es">Sansón</span>; <span title="it">Sansone</span>; <span title="ru">Самсон</span>; <span title="ja">サムソン (ヘンデル)</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="es">Sanson</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/1146708038800841599">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samson_(Handel)">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/1146708038800841599">1146708038800841599</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/no2005090440">no2005090440</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300065655">300065655</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13913107r">13913107r</a>
</td></tr>

<th>Composer

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>HWV 57
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IGH 433
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dt>Act I.
</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 1</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>1. Overture
</dd><dd>2. Recitative (Samson): This day, a solemn feast to Dagon held
</dd><dd>3. Chorus of Philistines: Awake the trumpet's lofty sound!
</dd><dd>4. Air (Philistine Woman): Ye men of Gaza, hither bring
<dl><dd>Chorus: Awake the trumpet's lofty sound!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>5. Air (Philistine): Loud as the thunder's awful voice
</dd><dd>6. Air (Philistine Woman): Then free from sorrow, free from thrall
<dl><dd>Chorus: Awake the trumpet's lofty sound!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>7. Recitative (Samson): Why by an angel was my birth foretold
</dd><dd>8. Air (Samson): Torments, alas, are not confin'd
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 2</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>9. Recitative (Micah): Oh, change beyond report, thought, or belief!
</dd><dd>10. Air (Micah): Oh, mirror of our fickle state!
</dd><dd>11. Recitative (Samson, Micah)
<dl><dd>Samson. Whom have I to complain of but myself<br />Micah. Matchless in might! once Israel’s glory<br />Samson. Welcome, my friends! <br />Micah. Which shall we first bewail <br />Samson. O loss of sight, of thee I most complain!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>12. Air (Samson): Total eclipse! No sun, no moon!
</dd><dd>13. Accompagnato (Micah): Since light so necessary is to life
</dd><dd>14. Chorus of Israelites: O first created beam! 
</dd><dd>15. Recitative (Samson, Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Samson. Ye see, my friends<br />Micah. The wisest men have err'd, and been deceiv'd<br />Samson. Oh that I had! Alas, fond wish, too late! <br />Micah. Here comes thy rev'rend sire, old Manoah<br />Samson. Alas! Another grief that name awakes.
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 3</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd>Manoah. Brethren and men of Dan, say, where is my son?<br />Micah. As signal now in low dejected state
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>16. Accompagnato (Manoah): Oh, miserable change!
</dd><dd>17. Recitative (Israelitish Man): Oh, ever failing trust
</dd><dd>18. Air (Israelitish Man): God of our fathers, what is man?
</dd><dd>19. Accompagnato (Manoah): The good we wish for, often proves our bane
</dd><dd>20. Air (Manoah): Thy glorious deeds inspir'd my tongue
</dd><dd>21. Recitative (Samson, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Samson: Justly these evils have befalI'n thy son<br />Manoah: Worse yet remains. <br />Samson: This have I done
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>22. Accompagnato (Samson): My griefs for this
</dd><dd>23. Air (Samson): Why does the God of lsrael sleep?
</dd><dd>24. Recitative (Micah): There lies our hope!
</dd><dd>25. Chorus of Israelites: Then shall they know
</dd><dd>26. Recitative (Manoah, Samson)
<dl><dd>Manoah. For thee, my dearest son<br />Samson. It should be so, to expiate my crime <br />Manoah. Be for thy fate contrite <br />Samson. Why should I live?
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>27. Accompagnato (Samson): My genial spirits droop
</dd><dd>28. Recitative (Micah): Then long eternity
</dd><dd>29. Air (Micah): Joys that are pure
</dd><dd>30. Chorus of Israelites: Then round about the starry throne
</dd><dt>Act II.
</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 1</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>31. Recitative (Manoah, Samson)
<dl><dd>Manoah. Despair not thus!<br />Samson. Where'er the liquid brook or fountain<br />Manoah. Trust yet in God! 
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>32. Air (Manoah): Just are the ways of God to man
</dd><dd>33. Recitative (Samson, Micah)
<dl><dd>Samson. My evils hopeless are!<br />Micah. Relieve Thy champion 
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>34. Air and Chorus (Micah, Israelites)
<dl><dd>Micah. Return, O God of hosts! Behold
</dd><dd>Israelites. To dust his glory they would tread, 
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 2</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>35. Recitative (Samson, Micah, Dalila)
<dl><dd>Micah. But who is this, that so bedeck'd and gay<br />Samson. My wife, my traitress?<br />Micah. She stands, and eyes thee fix'd<br />Dalila. With doubtful feet, and wav'ring resolution<br />Samson. Out, thou hyæna!<br />Dalila. I would not lessen my offence, yet beg<br />Samson. How cunningly the sorceress displays
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>36. Air (Philistine Woman / Dalila): With plaintive notes
</dd><dd>37. Recitative (Dalila, Samson)
<dl><dd>Dalila. Alas! Th'event was worse than I foresaw<br />Samson. Did love constrain thee? No, 'twas raging lust!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>38. Air (Samson): Your charms to ruin led the way
</dd><dd>39. Recitative (Dalila): Forgive what's done
</dd><dd>40. Air and Duet (Dalila, Philistine Woman)
<dl><dd>Dalila. My faith and truth, O Samson, prove,
</dd><dd>Philistine Woman. Her faith and truth
</dd><dd>41a. Chorus of Virgins: Her faith and truth
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>42. Air (Dalila): To fleeting pleasures
<dl><dd>41b. Chorus of Virgins: Her faith and truth
</dd><dd>Air (Dalila): How charming is domestic ease!
</dd><dd>41c. Chorus of Virgins: Her faith and truth
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>43. Recitative (Samson, Dalila)
<dl><dd>Samson. Ne'er think of that!<br />Dalila. Let me approach, at least<br />Samson. Not for thy life, lest fierce remembrance wake<br />Dalila. Thou art more deaf to pray'rs
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>44. Duet (Dalila, Samson): Traitor to love! I'll sue no more
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 3</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>45. Recitative (Micah, Samson)
<dl><dd>Micah. She's gone!<br />Samson. So let her go!
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>46. Air (Micah): It is not virtue, valour, wit
</dd><dd>47. Recitative (Samson): Favour'd of heaven is he
</dd><dd>48. Chorus of Israelites: To man God's universal law
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 4</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>49. Recitative (Micah, Harapha, Samson)
<dl><dd>Micah. No words of peace<br />Harapha. I come not, Samson, to condole thy chance<br />Samson. The way to know. were not to see<br />Harapha. Ha! Dost thou then already single me?<br />Samson. Boast not of what thou would'st have done<br />Harapha. The honour certain to have won from thee
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>50. Air (Harapha): Honour and arms
</dd><dd>51. Recitative (Samson): Put on your arms
</dd><dd>52. Air (Samson): My strength is from the living God
</dd><dd>53. Recitative (Harapha, Samson)
<dl><dd>Harapha.With thee, a man condemn'd<br />Samson. Cam'st thou for this, vain boaster?<br />Harapha. O Dagon! Can I hear this insolence
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>54. Duet (Samson, Harapha): Go, baffled coward; Presume not on thy God
</dd><dd>55. Recitative (Micah): Here lies the proof
</dd><dd>56. Chorus of Israelites: Hear, Jacob's God, Jehovah, hear!
</dd><dd>57. Recitative (Harapha): Dagon, arise, attend thy sacred feast!
</dd><dd>58. Air (A Philistine): To song and dance we give the day
</dd><dd>59. Chorus of Philistines: To song and dance we give the day
</dd><dd>60. Chorus of Israelites and Philistines: Fix'd in his everlasting seat
</dd><dt>Act II.
</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 1</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>61. Recitative (Micah, Samson, Harapha)
<dl><dd>Micah. More trouble is behind<br />Samson. I fear him not, nor all his giant brood<br />Harapha. Samson, to thee our lords thus bid me say<br />Samson. I am an Hebrew<br />Harapha. This answer will offend<br />Samson. Myself, my conscience and intemal peace!<br />Harapha. My message, giv'n with speed
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>62. Air (Harapha): Presuming slave, to move their wrath!
</dd><dd>63. Recitative (Micah, Samson)
<dl><dd>Micah. Reflect then. Samson<br />Samson. Shall I abuse this consecrated gift<br />Micah. How thou wilt here come 
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>64. Chorus of Israelites: With thunder arm'd, great God, arise!
</dd><dd>65. Recitative (Samson, Micah, Harapha)
<dl><dd>Samson. Be of good courage<br />Micah. In time thou hast resolv'd<br />Harapha. Samson, this second summons send our lords<br />Samson. Vain were their art if tried<br />Harapha. You thus may win the lords<br />Samson. In nothing I'll comply that's scandalous<br />Micah. So may'st thou act as serves His glory best<br />Samson. Let but that spirit
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>66. Accompagnato (Samson): Then shall I make Jehovah's glory
</dd><dd>67. Air (Samson): Thus when the sun from's wat'ry bed
</dd><dd>68. Accompagnato (Micah): With might endu'd above the sons of men
</dd><dd>69. Air and Chorus (Micah): The Holy One of Israel be thy guide
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 2</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>70. Recitative (Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Micah. Old Manoah, with youthful steps<br />Manoah. I come, my brethren
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>71. Air (Philistine): Great Dagon has subdu'd our foe
</dd><dd>72. Chorus of Philistines: Great Dagon has subdu'd our foe
</dd><dd>73. Recitative (Manoah, Micah)
<dl><dd>Manoah. What noise of joy was that?<br />Micah. They shout and sing<br />Manoah. Could my inheritance but ransom him<br />Micah. Sons care to nurse
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>74. Air (Manoah): How willing my paternal love
</dd><dd>75. Recitative (Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Micah. Your hopes of his deliv'ry seem not vain<br />Manoah. I know your friendly minds
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>76. Chorus of Philistines: Hear us, our God! Oh, hear our cry!
</dd><dd>77. Recitative (Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Micah. Noise call you this?<br />Manoah. Ruin indeed!<br />Micah. Thy son is rather slaying them  
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><i>Scene 3</i>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>78. Recitative (Messenger, Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Messenger. Where shall I run<br />Micah. The accident was loud<br />Messenger. Let me recover breath<br />Manoah. Tell us the sum (etc.)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>79. Air and Chorus (Micah, Israelites): Ye sons of lsrael, now lament,
</dd><dd>80. Recitative (Manoah): Proceed we hence to find his body
</dd><dd>81. Symphony: Dead March
</dd><dd>82. Recitative (Micah, Manoah)
<dl><dd>Micah. The body comes<br />Manoah. There shall all IsraeI's valiant youth resort
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>83. Air and Chorus (Manoah, Israelites): Glorious hero, may thy grave
</dd><dd>84. Solo and Chorus (Israelite Woman, Virgins)
<dl><dd>Israelite Woman. The virgins too shall on their feastful days
</dd><dd>Virgins. Bring the laurels, bring the bays,
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>85. Recitative (Manoah, Micah)
<dl><dd>Manoah. Come, come! No time for lamentation now<br />Micah. Why should we weep or wail
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>86. Air (Israelite Woman): Let the bright seraphim
</dd><dd>87. Chorus of Israelites: Let their celestial concerts all unite </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>

<td>1741
